<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g65140g44u03.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AstroNova Reports Record Sales for the </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Third Quarter of Fiscal 2016; Board of Directors Declares Regular Cash Dividend </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Reports 13th Consecutive Quarter of Growth; Achieves Double-Digit Increases in Orders and Backlog </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third-Quarter Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sales increased 7% to $24.8 million </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Net income of $1.3 million </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Backlog increased 39% from year-end to $16.8 million </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WEST WARWICK, RI &#150;November 25, 2015</B> &#151;
Astro-Med, Inc., d/b/a AstroNova (NASDAQ: ALOT), a leading manufacturer of data visualization technology for the aerospace, specialty printing, and test&nbsp;&amp; measurement markets, today reported third-quarter fiscal 2016 net sales of $24.8
million, a 7% increase year-on-year. Third-quarter net income was $1.3 million, or $0.18 per diluted share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We reported our 13<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of year-over-year top-line growth with double-digit percentage increases in orders and backlog,&#148; said Gregory A. Woods, the Company&#146;s President and Chief Executive
Officer. &#147;Domestic sales grew 8% for the quarter, while international sales were up more than 4%. International sales were tempered by the strong dollar, which lowered international sales by approximately $0.7 million. We continue to realize
the strategic benefits of our global expansion efforts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Demand in our QuickLabel Systems business drove record results for that segment, as sales
of labels, inks, and other consumables increased 27% from the prior year&#146;s third quarter,&#148; Woods continued. &#147;In response, we have recently added a third shift at our consumables plant in West Warwick, marking the first time in the
Company&#146;s 46-year history that we have operated one of our facilities on an around-the-clock basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In our Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement
segment, the integration of RITEC Inc.&#146;s ruggedized printer product line remains on schedule for completion by the end of the fiscal year. Our recent expansion in regions such as Southeast Asia has helped to build new relationships for our
Aerospace, Product Identification, and Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement products. We are excited about the many new opportunities for our businesses,&#148; Woods said. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g65140g54g22.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit for the third quarter of fiscal 2016 was $10.1 million, or 41.0% of sales, compared with $10.1
million, or 43.9% of sales, for the year-earlier period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income for the third quarter of fiscal 2016 was $1.3 million, or $0.18 per diluted share,
compared with net income of $1.6 million, or $0.20 per diluted share, in the same period of fiscal 2015. There were approximately $0.5 million in transition charges associated with the RITEC acquisition incurred during the third quarter of fiscal
2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash and cash equivalents at October&nbsp;31, 2015 were $22.5 million, compared with $23.1 million at year-end fiscal 2015. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third-Quarter Business Segment Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>QuickLabel Systems </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Board of Directors Declares Regular Quarterly Dividend </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&nbsp;23, 2015, the Directors of AstroNova declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.07 per share. The dividend, which represents a cash
dividend of $0.28 per share on an annualized basis, is payable on January&nbsp;4, 2016, to shareholders of record as of the close of business on December&nbsp;18, 2015. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Demand for our data visualization products continues to be strong, boosting our orders and backlog. From both a financial and an operational perspective
we are well positioned in fiscal 2016 and beyond,&#148; Woods said. &#147;We remain focused on deploying our AstroNova Operating System to achieve continuous improvements in product quality, manufacturing efficiency, delivery, cost, and
growth.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third-Quarter FY 2016 Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova will conduct an investor conference call at 9:00 a.m. EST today. Investors can participate in the conference call by dialing 888-403-8872 (U.S. and
Canada) or 719-457-2693 (International) with passcode 963533. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Please join the call at least five minutes prior to the start time. You can also hear a
live webcast of the call by accessing the Investors section of AstroNova&#146;s website, <U>www.astronovainc.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Following the live broadcast, an
audio webcast replay of the call will be available at www.astronovainc.com. A telephone replay of the conference call will be available for seven days by dialing 888-203-1112 (U.S. and Canada) or 719-457-0820 (International) with passcode 9749359.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Astro-Med, Inc., d/b/a AstroNova,
is a global leader in data visualization technology delivering accuracy, efficiency, speed, and performance across a range of end-user markets. The Company&#146;s products include color label printers and consumables sold under the QuickLabel brand,
ruggedized printers and networking products for aerospace and defense applications, as well as test&nbsp;&amp; measurement products sold under the AstroNova brand.&nbsp;Astro-Med, Inc.&nbsp;is a member of the Russell Microcap<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Index. Additional information is available by visiting&nbsp;www.astronovainc.com. </P>
